class="content-container site-container"><div id="main" class="site-main"><div class="content-wrap"><article id="post-69" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-69 page type-page status-publish hentry grow-content-main"><div class="entry-content-wrap"><div class="entry-content single-content"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id69_d04ef2-cf alignfull kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-layout-overlay kt-row-overlay-normal"></div><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kb-theme-content-width"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column69_546715-6f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div style="height:57px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><h1 class="kt-adv-heading69_f228e1-8c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_f228e1-8c">Adventurous family travel in Europe that works in the school holidays</h1><p></p></div></div></div></div><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id69_9271ab-f6 alignfull has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-row kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kb-theme-content-width"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column69_b53d78-0f kb-section-dir-vertical inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="kt-adv-heading69_6e10c6-f6 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_6e10c6-f6">I’m Bea (pronounced Bee). I’ve been working in the travel and outdoor industry since 2006, and I now use everything I’ve learned to help families plan adventurous, independent trips in Europe – which work in the school holidays, without theme parks, tour groups, or canned entertainment.</p><p class="kt-adv-heading69_953a1d-c1 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_953a1d-c1">In 2025 I was named one of Cycling UK’s <em><a href="https://www.cyclinguk.org/biography/bea-searle" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">100 Women in Cycling</a></em>, an award celebrating women who inspire others to get outdoors on two wheels. It’s a huge honour; cycling has shaped so much of my life and still guides the way I travel with my own family today.</p><p>I started <strong>Wild Bee Outdoors</strong> after decades of planning our own trips. I’m always looking for the good stuff that’s easy to miss:<br>🚲 traffic-free cycling routes and family-friendly hiking trails<br>🌲 free or low-cost outdoor adventures<br>🏡 simple places to stay that help you get to know a place, not remain apart from it<br>🚆 <a href="/train-trips">Train routes</a> (overnight trains are my favourite), and local buses that take you straight to trailheads and mountain villages</p></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column69_c3b159-5b kb-section-dir-vertical inner-column-2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image69_3ea03d-5a"><figure class="aligncenter size-full kb-image-is-ratio-size"><div class="kb-is-ratio-image kb-image-ratio-port34"><img decoding="async" width="901" height="900" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20901%20900'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="A woman and two kids smile while walking on a wooded trail in the mountains, dressed in tie-dye shirts and hiking gear. A serene scene that reflects the joy of travelling adventurously as a solo parent with kids in nature." class="kb-img wp-image-4539" data-lazy-srcset="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited.webp 901w, https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited-300x300.webp 300w, https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited-150x150.webp 150w, https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited-768x767.webp 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 901px) 100vw, 901px" data-lazy-src="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="901" height="900" src="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited.webp" alt="A woman and two kids smile while walking on a wooded trail in the mountains, dressed in tie-dye shirts and hiking gear. A serene scene that reflects the joy of travelling adventurously as a solo parent with kids in nature." class="kb-img wp-image-4539" srcset="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited.webp 901w, https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited-300x300.webp 300w, https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited-150x150.webp 150w, https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Hiking-on-an-Austrian-Farm-Stay-edited-768x767.webp 768w" sizes="(max-width: 901px) 100vw, 901px" /></noscript></div></figure></div></div></div></div></div><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id69_ef5036-f5 alignfull has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kb-theme-content-width"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column69_5ed39c-00 kb-section-dir-vertical inner-column-2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p>I know how hard it can be to:</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>find reliable information (often in another language)</li><li>turn scattered ideas into a coherent, bookable itinerary</li><li>plan trips with real adventure – <a href="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/hut-to-hut-hiking/" data-type="page" data-id="1157">hut to hut hiking</a>, <a href="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/multi-day-cycling/" data-type="page" data-id="1140">multi-day cycling</a>, <a href="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/family-skiing-les-arcs/" data-type="page" data-id="3719">skiing in family-friendly resorts</a> – without joining a tour</li><li>feel confident that a route or trip really will work for <em>your</em> family</li></ul><p>Everything I share here is based on trips we’ve actually done. I provide route notes, maps, transport guidance and practical advice so you can travel independently and confidently – exploring the Alps and beyond at your own pace, often without needing a car.</p><p>If you love the idea of family travel that’s outdoorsy, culturally curious, and properly adventurous – but still the sort that fits into real life and school holidays – you’re in the right place.</p><p>And if you’re curious about what inspired this blog and why it can help with your own adventures, you can read more <a href="https://wildbeeoutdoors.co.uk/about/" data-type="page" data-id="2">here</a>.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column69_972fe8-45"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="kt-adv-heading69_629d00-c3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_629d00-c3"><strong>Start your research here:</strong></h2></div></div><ul data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_b55bcd-ca">Spain</h3><div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns69_056e26-3e"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn69_eabbb2-c2 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="/spain" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Read more</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h2 class="kt-adv-heading69_0a8651-bb wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_0a8651-bb"><strong>Disclaimer</strong></h2><p class="kt-adv-heading69_09e9f0-3e wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading69_09e9f0-3e">I&#8217;m not a mountain guide, just a passionate hiker and cyclist. I want you to use the information I provide here, but please, always double-check your plans. Trails can change and snow can stick around even in the height of summer. Take ownership of your adventure. Do your homework, plan your routes carefully, double check the weather forecast, and never head out unprepared. Wear sturdy, waterproof footwear, pack essentials like maps, navigation apps, food, water, cash, a phone and a battery pack. The mountains can be unpredictable!</p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-medium"><img decoding="async" width="240" height="300"
